For large text (24px or larger, or 18pt bold and above), WCAG Level AA requires a minimum contrast ratio of 3:1.\n\n## UI Components & Graphics\n\nWCAG 2.1 introduced Success Criterion 1.4.11 Non-text Contrast (Level AA), which requires visual information for user interface components and graphical objects to have a contrast ratio of at least 3:1 against adjacent colors. This applies to buttons, form fields, icons, and other interactive elements.\n\n## Mobile Considerations\n\nAccording to WCAG Mobile guidelines, mobile devices are more likely to be used in varied environments including outdoors where glare heightens the importance of good contrast and may compound challenges for users with low vision. Small screens and varied lighting conditions make contrast even more critical for readability on mobile.\n\n## Key Requirements Summary\n\n- **Normal text**: 4.5:1 minimum\n- **Large text**: 3:1 minimum  \n- **UI components/graphics**: 3:1 minimum against adjacent colors\n- **Enhanced (AAA level)**: 7:1 for normal text, 4.5:1 for large text\n\nThe minimum values are absolute - 2.99:1 does not meet the 3:1 requirement, and 4.49:1 does not meet the 4.5:1 requirement.\n\nThese standards remain current for 2025 and apply to all digital interfaces, including mobile applications and responsive websites."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d52eefdd-66db-418a-872b-d2b8f6531ff1","uuid":"a2c2c9e1-2e66-46a6-9850-7eeeae7fc803"}

A common solution is giving the inner container of the modal a fixed viewport height like maxHeight: \"90vh\".\n\n## Calculation with calc()\n\nThe CSS approach uses max-height:calc(100vh - 125px) to account for padding and header heights. For the modal body, use calc() function to calculate desired height - for example, max-height: calc(80vh - 140px) for occupying 80vh of the viewport, reduced by the size of header + footer in pixels.\n\n## Mobile-Specific Guidelines\n\nDialogs should maintain a minimum 48dp distance from the leading and trailing edges of a screen, and on small screens, dialogs scale vertically until reaching 48dp from the screen's top and bottom edge.\n\n## General Principles\n\nIdeally the modal is as tall as need be to contain its contents, but no taller, and the viewport is taller than the modal.
